│    266   [^13]: The Bodhisattvas' verse of rejoicing employs the traditional formula of accepting the      │
│          Buddha's teaching with "excellent, excellent." Their specific rejoicing in the ease of teaching   │
│          and the trustworthiness of the Buddha's wisdom establishes that what the Buddha teaches is        │
│          verifiable and worthy of reliance.                                                                │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    377 -                                                                                                   │
│    267   [^14]: The Buddha's praise of those who can "generate hearts of rejoicing" establishes that faith │
│          and confidence in the teaching itself are precious achievements. Not all beings spontaneously     │
│          rejoice; this response is itself a sign of spiritual development.                                 │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    379 -                                                                                                   │
│    268   [^15]: Maitreya's realization that "such an assembly has never been seen before" establishes that │
│          this phenomenon is genuinely extraordinary—unprecedented in his vast experience. This sets up the │
│          dramatic need for explanation.                                                                    │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    381 -                                                                                                   │
│    269   [^16]: Maitreya's verse question is one of the Lotus Sutra's greatest poetic achievements. It     │
│          catalogs the mystery from every angle: who are these beings, where did they come from, how many   │
│          are there, what Dharma did they learn, whose path do they follow? The accumulation of unanswered  │
│          questions builds momentum toward the answer coming in Chapter 16.                                 │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    383 -                                                                                                   │
│    270   [^17]: The note that the division-bodies of Shakyamuni throughout the cosmos heard his voice      │
│          establishes that this moment is **cosmic in scope**—not merely local but reverberating across     │
│          infinite worlds. All Buddhas and their attendants are aware of what is occurring.                 │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    385 -                                                                                                   │
│    271   [^18]: Each Buddha's attendants ask the same question their respective Buddha-lords do, showing   │
│          universal perplexity. The mystery is not local but cosmic.                                        │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    387 -                                                                                                   │
│    272   [^19]: The instruction to "wait for Maitreya's answer" establishes Maitreya as the **cosmic       │
│          representative** whose question speaks for all beings. His answer will be an answer for the       │
│          entire universe.                                                                                  │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    389 -                                                                                                   │
│    273   [^20]: The Buddha's call to "put on the armor of diligent effort" and "establish firm resolve"    │
│          prepares for the revelation that will challenge conventional understanding of time and causality. │
│          Such radical teaching requires spiritual preparation.                                             │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    391 -                                                                                                   │
│    274   [^21]: The phrase "reveal the wisdom of all Buddhas, the supernatural powers of all Buddhas, the  │
│          lion's roar-power of all Buddhas" establishes that what is about to be revealed concerns          │
│          **ultimate reality**, not secondary matters. This is the apex of teaching.                        │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    393 -                                                                                                   │
│    275   [^22]: The verse emphasizes that the teaching to come is unprecedented ("what you have never      │
│          heard before"), beyond conceptual understanding ("beyond discrimination"), and requires undivided │
│          faith. These three preparations show that Chapter 16's revelation requires special readiness.     │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    395 -                                                                                                   │
│    276   [^23]: The statement that these Bodhisattvas "dwell beneath the surface of this Sahā world-realm, │
│          in the empty space within the earth itself" is crucial. It suggests an interior rather than       │
│          exterior location—they practice in the depths of consciousness, the underground of the            │
│          world-system.                                                                                     │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    397 -                                                                                                   │
│    277   [^24]: The characterization of these disciples emphasizes their solitude, non-attachment, and     │
│          focus on wisdom. They are not gathered in crowds seeking worldly benefits but dwelling in the     │
│          interior depths, pursuing the profound Dharma continuously.                                       │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    399 -                                                                                                   │
│    278   [^25]: The verse's declaration "I have cultivated and taught these beings for very long ages      │
│          indeed" provides the bridge to Chapter 16. It plants the question: just how long is "very long    │
│          ages"? The answer will be: infinite eons.                                                         │
│    ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ │
│    401 -                                                                                                   │
│    402 - [^26]: **Revelation versus Creation** is a fundamental theological distinction. In creation       │
│        theology, God creates newness ex nihilo (from nothing). In revelation theology, what exists is      │
│        brought to manifestation or recognition. Buddhism inclines toward revelation: the Buddha awakens to │
│        what is, not creates what wasn't.                                                                   │
│    403 -                                                                                                   │
│    404 - [^27]: The **underworld as practice-ground** appears in various mystical traditions. In Dante,    │
│        the descent into hell becomes the path to enlightenment. In Chinese philosophy, the depths          │
│        represent the uncarved potential. The Bodhisattvas' dwelling beneath the earth suggests             │
│        enlightenment is achieved through depth and interiority.                                            │
│    405 -                                                                                                   │
│    406 - [^28]: The **mystery as pedagogical tool** is sophisticated teaching method. Rather than stating  │
│        the answer directly, the Buddha creates conditions where the question becomes undeniable. The       │
│        revelation is more transformative when it resolves genuine perplexity.                              │
│    407 -                                                                                                   │
│    408 - [^29]: The **four qualities of conduct** model a comprehensive practice path. Superior Conduct    │
│        establishes excellence; Boundless extends it infinitely; Pure purifies intention; Stable grounds    │
│        the achievement. Together they form a complete spiritual architecture.                              │
│    409 -                                                                                                   │
│    410 - [^30]: The **infinite multiplicity within unity** is expressed through the numbers. Each          │
│        Bodhisattva leads others yet all are unified in serving the teaching. Individual manifestation and  │
│        cosmic unity coexist paradoxically.                                                                 │
│    411 -                                                                                                   │
│    412 - [^31]: **Reality exceeds quantification** is established through the deliberate frustration of    │
│        mathematical calculation. The attempt to number the Bodhisattvas fails inherently. This teaches     │
│        that ultimate reality cannot be captured through conceptual or mathematical means alone.            │
│    413 -                                                                                                   │
│    414 - [^32]: **Temporal relativity** appears in both modern physics (Einstein) and in mystical          │
│        experience (contemplatives report that deep states feel timeless). The Buddha's consciousness       │
│        operates in a different temporal frame, making fifty eons pass as half a day.                       │
│    415 -                                                                                                   │
│    416 - [^33]: **Intentional ambiguity** is a sophisticated teaching device. By leaving the statement     │
│        open to misinterpretation, the Buddha creates conditions for progressive revelation. The listener   │
│        first hears one meaning, then recognizes a deeper truth, and the teaching becomes an active process │
│        rather than passive reception.                                                                      │
│    417 -                                                                                                   │
│    418 - ---                                                                                               │
